### 前言

《英语（二）考试大纲》明确规定：“考生应掌握词汇的语言知识，并能在特定情境下的语言活动中加以有效运用。”考试大纲重点考查的是词汇的基本知识和情景运用。

词汇的基本知识主要包括：（1）单词的常见释义；（2）单词的习惯用法，如固定搭配、固定表达等；（3）单词之间的语义关系，如近义关系、反义关系等。

考研英语试题分三部分，包括英语知识运用（即完形填空），阅读理解（包括阅读A、阅读B和阅读C）和写作。我们在深刻领会考试大纲对词汇考查要求的基础上，以“攻克题型词汇”为纲，将精选的真题词汇按照题型分类，再依据词性与词义数量将每个题型的词汇进一步分为“单词性单词义”“单词性多词义”“多词性单词义”和“多词性多词义”四个子类，内容由易到难，详略得当，直击重点，考点，真正实现背词减负。

## 一、编写思路

我们统计了2010年以来考研英语（二）真题文章中出现的所有单词，按照词汇难度进行了分级处理，即五级（初中）词、高中词、四级词、六级词、考研词、派生词和复合词，精选出1450个作为“基础过关词”放入分册，零频词汇（约1000个）也纳入分册，其余真题考查过的词汇纳入主书。关于“派生词”和“复合词”的分类处理原则：只要该词在考试大纲中出现，我们就将其归入各自的级别分类中；若该词未在考试大纲中出现，则将其单独分类注释。

主书分为以下六章内容：

（1）第一章：必考词。本章词汇为四题型共有词，我们根据其难度分为“基础词”和“进阶词”两个单元。基础词部分我们仅罗列词头、词频、音标、词性和释义，而进阶词部分需要重点记忆，因而附有较为详细的讲解。

(2) 第二章：以完形填空为中心。本章词汇下分为两个单元，第一单元为“两题型共有词”，包括完形分别与阅读 A、阅读 B 以及阅读 C 的共有词；第二单元为“交叉共有词”，包括完形—阅读 A+阅读 B、完形—阅读 A—阅读 C 以及完形+阅读 B—阅读 C 的共有词。

（3）第三章：以阅读理解为中心。本章词汇下分为两个单元，第一单元为“阅读 A+阅读 B-阅读 C 共有词”；第二单元为“交叉共有词”，包括阅读 A-阅读 B、阅读 A-阅读 C 以及阅读 B-阅读 C 的共有词。本章词汇在真题阅读理解版块多次考查，需重点记忆。

（4）第四章：专项词。本章词汇词数较多，下分为四个单元，分别是完形填空、阅读 A、阅读 B 和阅读 C 这四个题型的独有词，有助于学生分门别类地记忆各题型单词。

（5）第五章：写作表达积累。本章词汇下分四个单元，第一单元“话题常用词汇”归纳了近15年来真题写作范文中出现的常见词汇、高频短语以及亮点表达，并按照词义划分成小类，可以有效帮助考生洞悉真题；第二单元“框架搭建词汇”着眼于不同语用功能的词汇，掌握此部分词汇及相关搭配有助于构建完整的行文脉络，并提升行文的流畅度；第三单元“词句多样表达”引导考生通过变换词性和使用不同词汇提升用词的丰富性，通过变换句式和使用特殊句型来提升造句的灵活性；第四单元“热点话题预测”补充高频及热点表述，有助于考生更好地把握命题趋势。

（6）第六章：超纲词。本章词汇分为“学术专业词”和“通用实用词”两个单元。学术专业词多为概念性词汇，学生只需掌握释义即可；通用实用词大多值得记忆，可能在今后考试中再次出现，学生需要尽量掌握。

## 二、编写体例

我们在撰写详细注释的词条时仅收录真题考查过的义项，优先使用最新的真题语料。词条内增加了词频和星级（词频1～5标★☆☆，6～10标★★☆，10以上标★★★），学生可根据词频等级及自身需求重点记忆。在词条下方，我们给出了真题中其他包含该单词的短语或例句（ $ \underline{\text{真}} $）、题源外刊中选取的例句（ $ \underline{\text{例}} $）或权威词典中列出的常见搭配（ $ \underline{\text{扩}} $），以及该单词的常见近/反义词（ $ \underline{\text{近反}} $）或真题考查过的派生词（ $ \underline{\text{派}} $），帮助考生在真实语境中记忆单词，同时积累词汇的常见用法。

## 三、赠品分册

本书除了主书之外，还包括基础过关1450词、零频词汇分级汇编和核心词汇精缩本。

##### （1）基础过关1450词

基础过关1450词包括入门必备900词、进阶必备520词和题干必考30词。其中，入门必备900词为英语学习的入门级词汇，包含二级（小学）、五级（初中）和部分难度较低的高中词汇，考生可快速扫过、查缺补漏。进阶必备520词为考研英语常考话题的通用词汇，内部根据难度进一步分为初级（120词）、中级（150词）、高级（250词），层层递进，便于考生循序渐进、逐级突破；掌握该部分词汇有助于考生扫清话题通用的基础词汇，减少阅读障碍。题干必考30词为历年考研英语题干中的高频词汇，掌握该部分词汇有助于考生读懂题干、准确审题。

##### （2）零频词汇分级汇编

零频词汇（约1000词）内容涵盖真题中尚未考查的大纲词汇，我们根据单词的难易程度进行分级、分类，各层级之间区分显著，便于读者由易到难、逐级突破，帮助考生有选择性地识记词汇。

##### （3）核心词汇精缩本

大多数考生需要抽出碎片化时间随时随地背诵单词，而主书比较厚重，难以携带，为了满足学生的这一需求，我们将主书中的所有词头编排成易携带的精缩本，其选词及单词顺序与主书完全一致，奇数页提供词头和音标，偶数页相应位置给出词性和词义，方便考生检测记忆成果，并对遗忘的单词进行巩固。

使用本书时，考生可先对基础过关1450词一扫而过；然后深入学习主书内容，其间可随身携带核心词汇精缩本加强巩固；掌握好主书内容之后再熟悉零频词汇。

最后、预祝各位考生成功上岸！

张剑锋

##### V. 压垮；使应接不暇

②令人不知所措的 $ ^{1} $

overwhelmingly [əʊvəˈwelmɪŋli]

## 二、单词性多词义(12词)

（一）名词（4词）

#### 1. 高中词(3词)

concern $ ^{16} $ ★★★ [kənˈsɜːn]

###### n. ①担心；忧虑 $ ^{13} $

真 there are concerns that... 有人担心……

concern about real grass supply

对“天然草坪供应(不足)”的担心

(be) grounded in health concerns

基于健康(方面的)担心

raise security and privacy concerns

引发安全和隐私(方面的)忧虑

 $ \underline{扩} $ concerns over inflation 对通货膨胀的忧虑 address voters' concerns about the economy 设法解决选民们对经济的忧虑

近 anxiety [æŋˈzaɪəti] n. 担心；忧虑 $ ^{4} $

②担心的事；关切的事

真 a national concern 一件举国关切之事

be basically private concerns 从根本上讲是私事

the indispensable supporter 不可或缺的支撑物

Daily schedules are  $ \underline{\text{indispensable}} $ to studying. 每日计划表对学习是 $ \underline{\text{不可或缺的}} $.

扩 an indispensable tool for solving these problems 解决这些问题的必要工具

近 essential [ɪˈsenʃl] a. 完全必要的；必不可少的

反 dispensable [di'spensəbl] a. 可有可无的

vulnerable $ ^{3} $ ★☆☆ [ˈvʌlənərəbl]

###### a. 易受攻击的；易受伤害的

 $ \underline{真} $ leave much of the Internet vulnerable 使互联网的大部分地方易受攻击

These jobs are so  $ \underline{\text{vulnerable}} $ to technology. 这些工作在技术面前如此 $ \underline{\text{不堪一击}} $。

扩 be in a vulnerable position 处于易受攻击的位置

近 susceptible [səˈseptəbl] a. 易受伤害的

反 invulnerable [inˈvʌlnərəbl] a. 不会受伤害的

feasible $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ [ˈfiːzəbl]

###### a. 可行的；行得通的

真 How  $ \underline{\text{feasible}} $ is this vision? 这一愿景的 $ \underline{\text{可行性}} $如何？

扩 a feasible plan/suggestion/idea

可行的计划/建议/想法

look for a feasible way 寻找可行的办法

近 practicable ['præktɪkəbl] a. 可行的；行得通的

反 unfeasible [ʌnˈfiːzəbl] a. 不可行的；难实现的

principal $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ [ˈprɪnsəpl]

###### a. 主要的；最重要的

真 a principal energy source 一个主要的能源来源

扩 the principal reason 主要的原因 the country's principal cities 该国的主要城市

近 main [meɪn] a. 主要的；最重要的+

反 minor [ˈmɪnə(r)] a. 较小的；次要的

派 principally [ˈprɪnsəpli] ad. 主要地

## （四）副词（8词）

#### 1. 高中词(3词)

therefore $ ^{9} $ ★ ★ ☆ [ˈðeəfɔː(r)]

##### ad. 因此；所以

 $ \underline{\text{Therefore}} $，everyone needs to find their extra value.因此，所有人都需要找到自身的额外价值。

 $ \underline{扩} $ fail to get funding and therefore abandon the project 未能筹到资金,因此放弃计划

 $ \overline{\text{近}} $ consequently ['kɒnsɪkwəntli] ad. 因此；所以

somewhat $ ^{3} $ ★☆☆ [ˈsʌm wɒt]

##### ad. 有点；有几分

真 be somewhat overweight 有几分超重

be somewhat more optimistic 更乐观一点

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ look somewhat different

看起来有些不同

become somewhat unpredictable

变得有些不可预测

 $ \overline{近} $ slightly [ˈslætlɪ] ad. 略微；稍微

nevertheless $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ [nevadeʒles]

##### ad. 然而；尽管如此

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $  $ \underline{\text{Nevertheless}} $，the affordable housing situation is desperate.然而，经济适用房的形势却很严峻

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ old-fashioned but nevertheless useful methods

过时但仍然有用的方法

 $ \underline{\text{近}} $ nonetheless [ˈnʌndəˈles] ad.然而；尽管如此

#### 2. 考研词(1词)

conversely $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ [ˈkɒnvɜːsli]

ad. 相反地；反过来

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $  $ \underline{\text{Conversely}} $，if homework matters... $ \underline{\text{相反}} $，如果家庭作业很重要……

 $ \underline{\text{折}} $ Nobody is all bad, nor, conversely, all good.没有人是彻头彻尾的坏人，相反地，也没有完完全全的好人：

反 likewise ['laɪkwɑɪz]

ad. 同样地；以相似方式地

#### 3. 派生词(4词)

temporarily $ ^{6} $ ★★☆ [ˈtemprərəli]

ad. 短暂地；暂时地

 $ \underline{\text{stay}} $ in a foreign country temporarily

短暂居留国外

temporarily lower carbon-carrying capacity

暂时降低碳承载能力

 $ \underline{扩} $ be temporarily unavailable 暂时不可用

temporarily halt the civil war

暂时中止内战

近 briefly [ˈbriːfli] ad. 短暂地；暂时地

 $ \underline{反} $ permanently [ˈpɜːmənəntli] ad.永久地；长久地

workplace 工作场所中有人类参与的必要性

 $ \underline{\text{近}} $ intense [in'tens] a.激烈的

###### a. ①深邃的；理解深刻的

 $ \underline{真} $ The insight is a  $ \underline{\text{profound}} $ one. 这是一种 $ \underline{\text{深刻的}} $见解。

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ develop a profound understanding of science 对科学形成深刻的理解

##### ②巨大的；深切的

profound changes in society 社会的巨大变革 profound disagreement on the cloning technique 关于克隆技术的巨大分歧

漲 profoundly [prəˈfaʊndli] ad. 极大地；深刻地

两种相互排斥的选择

n.<put/place/set a ~ on>重视;珍视

##### 移开；去掉

ad. 的确；确实

ad. 最终；最后

真 will eventually bring costs down 最终会拉低成本 will benefit homeowners eventually

最终会使房主受益

 $ \overline{近} $ finally [ˈfaɪnəli] ad. 最后；终于

 $ \underline{反} $ initially [ɪˈnɪʃəli] ad. 最初；起初

moreover $ ^{3} $ ★☆☆ [mɔːrˈəʊvə(r)]

ad. 此外；而且

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $  $ \underline{\text{Moreover}} $，we are grieving various kinds of loss.  $ \underline{\text{此外}} $，我们要为各种失去而伤心。

 $ \underline{近} $ besides [br'saɪdz] ad.此外；而且

##### ①选择；较喜欢

反 object [əbˈdʒekt] v. 反对；不赞成 $ ^{2} $ n. ①支持；赞成 $ ^{4} $

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $ in favor of the gap year 支持间隔年

avoid interacting with other human beings

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ interact with other scientists at the seminar room 在研讨室和其他科学家互动交流

近 communicate [kəˈmjuːnɪkeɪt] v. 交流；沟通²

派 interaction [ɪntərˈækʃn] n. 交流；互动 $ ^{7} $

②相互影响；相互作用

 $ \underline{真} $ Firms are now studying how genes  $ \underline{\text{interact}} $. 各企业当前正在研究基因间如何 $ \underline{\text{相互作用}} $.

 $ \underline{扩} $ interact with the skin's natural chemicals 和皮肤(上)的天然化学物质相互作用

派 interaction [ˌɪntərˈækʃn] n. 相互影响；相互作用 $ ^{2} $

capture $ ^{3} $ ★☆☆ [ˈkæptʃə(r)]

##### v. ①引起(注意、想象、兴趣) $ ^{2} $

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $ capture a reader 吸引读者 try to capture sb's attention 试图吸引某人的注意

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ capture the interest of teenagers

引起青少年的兴趣

use toys to capture the imagination of younger audiences 用玩具来引发小观众的想象力

pack $ ^{5} $ ★☆☆ [pæk]

##### v.①塞进；挤进

真 I truly believe that once you get that first word out everything else will just  $ \underline{\text{flow}} $.我坚信,一旦你将第一句话说出口,其余的(话)将会 $ \underline{\text{顺畅而行}} $。

扩 make the talk flow 使谈话顺畅进行

#### 1. 高中词(4词)

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ extend a deadline 延长最后期限

extend the life of the car 延长汽车寿命

stretch $ ^{3} $ ★☆☆ [stretf]

##### 连续

 $ \underline{真} $ a tradition of painting stretching from...to...

从……延续到……的绘画传统

 $ \underline{扩} $ stretch into a second week 延续到第二周

an artistic work that stretched over two years 一件历时两年完成的艺术品

 $ \underline{近} $ prolong [prəˈlɒŋ] v. 延长；延续

反 shorten [ˈʃɔːtn] v. (使)变短,缩短

②延伸;绵延

 $ \underline{真} $ a kind of bird living on stretching grasslands

一种栖息于绵延草原上的鸟类

 $ \underline{扩} $ stretch across the horizon 在地平线上延伸开来

近 extend [ɪkˈstend] v. 延伸(距离) $ ^{1} $

③伸展；舒展

真 stretch at home 在家进行伸展（运动）

 $ \underline{扩} $ stretch lazily 伸懒腰

stretch the leg muscles 伸展腿部肌肉

近 spread [spied] v. 张开；伸开

demonstrate $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ ['demənstreit]

##### v. ①表露；表现出

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $ demonstrate equal curiosity about other views 对他人的观点表现出同样的好奇心  $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ demonstrate self-control 表现出自制力 demonstrate an ability to meet deadlines 表现出如期完成任务的能力

 $ \underline{\text{近}} $ manifest [maenifest] v.表明；清楚地展示

反 hide [haɪd] v. 掩盖；隐瞒 $ ^{1} $

②说明；证明

真 demonstrate the intuitive nature of the social processing 证明对“社会(信息)处理”的直觉性

 $ \underline{扩} $ be demonstrated to be false 被证明是错误的

demonstrate some of the difficulties sb faces

说明某人面临的一些困难

 $ \overline{近} $ prove [pruv] v. 证明；证实

press $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ [pres]

v. ①按；压

 $ \underline{真} $ press a lever 按下控制杆

扩 press a button 按下按钮

press down hard on the gas pedal

用力踩下油门踏板

②<-- forward>努力前行

 $ \underline{真} $ press forward 努力前行

 $ \underline{扩} $ press forward in spite of the snow

尽管下雪依然努力前行

press forward and continue the journey

努力前行,继续旅程

#### 2. 四级词(1词)

impose $ ^{9} $ ★★☆ [imˈpəʊz]

##### v. ①推行；强制实行

真 impose stricter regulations 实行更严格的规定 impose a flat, across-the-board rule

实行一项呆板的、一刀切的规定

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ impose additional tax on fuel 对燃油征收附加税

②迫使；造成

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $ impose a heavier burden on immigrants 对移民造成更大的负担

 $ \underline{扩} $ impose enormous pressures on sb 对某人造成巨大的压力

近 force [fɔːs] v. 强迫；迫使

###### n.（贸易和经济活动的）激增，繁荣

#### 3. 考研词(2词)

 $ \underline{近} $ wealth [welθ] n. 大量；丰富

反 deficiency [dɪˈfɪnsi] n. 缺少；不足

 $ \underline{\text{近}} $ define [di'fain] v. 闯明；明确

##### ad. 同样地；类似地

 $ \underline{\text{Likewise}} $，among the elderly，being somewhat overweight is often an indicator of good health.  $ \underline{\text{同样地}} $，在老年人中，有几分超重往往是身体健康的标志。

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ likewise track the birds' eye movements 同样追踪鸟类的眼球运动

 $ \underline{\text{近}} $ similarly ['simələli] ad.相似地;类似地 $ ^{1} $  $ \underline{\text{反}} $ conversely ['kɒnvɜːsli] ad.相反地;反过来 $ ^{2} $

 $ \underline{真} $ be undoubtedly very tricky 确实很棘手

无疑是个有勇气的人

近 certainly [ˈsɜːtnli] ad. 确定地；肯定地

a helicopter pilot 直升机驾驶员

不知怎么地看上去变了

## 二、单词性多词义(47词)

（一）名词（24词）

1. 高中词(10词)

climate $ ^{17} $ ★★ [klaimət]

###### n. ①气候 $ ^{16} $

真 global climate change 全球气候变化 sponsor research on climate

为气候研究提供资金

help to fight climate change

有助于对抗气候变化

the positive impact on the climate

对气候的积极影响

②<~ off>衍生

例 Meanwhile, new legal cases continue to  $ \underline{\text{spin off}} $ from New York's redistricting stories.与此同时,新的法律案件继续从纽约的选区重划事件中 $ \underline{\text{衍生}} $出来. (2022 The New York Times)

 $ \underline{\text{扩}} $ spin off new commercial technologies

衍生出新的商业技术

products spinning off from bestsellers

从畅销书衍生出的产品

split $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ [split]

##### v.①(使)分开,分解

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $ split kids, or adults, into ever-tinier categories  

将儿童或者成年人细分为更小的类别

 $ \underline{扩} $ split a farm into 5 lots 将农田划分为5块

 $ \overline{\mathrm{近}} $ divide [dr'vaɪd] v.(使)分开,分成 $ ^{9} $

反 combine [kəmˈbain] v. (使)结合,组合 $ ^{3} $

②分配;分摊

真 be evenly split for A and B  

被平均分配给 A 和 B

 $ \underline{扩} $ split the cost 分摊费用

 $ \underline{近} $ share [ʃeə(r)] v.分摊；分配 $ ^{1} $

#### 3. 派生词(1词)

maximise/-ize $ ^{3} $ ★ ☆ ☆ [ˈmæksmaɪz]

##### v.①充分利用；最大限度地利用

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $ think of time as a resource to be maximised  

把时间看作是一种要充分利用的资源

充分利用机会

maximize the experience of specialists 充分利用专家的经验

##### ②使增加到最大限度

 $ \underline{\text{真}} $ maximize one's contribution to retirement account 按照最高标准缴纳某人的退休金

 $ \underline{扩} $ try to maximize profits 试图使利润最大化

反 minimise/-ize ['minmaɪz] v.使减少到最低限度

#### 3. 六级词(1词)

#### 11. 指令：执行令

V. 强制要求 $ ^{2} $

真 the proposed mandate 已提交的指令

扩 furniture placement 家具的摆放

## 三、多词性单词义（1词）

（一）名兼动（1词）

1. 高中词(1词)

blog $ ^{3} $ ★☆☆ [blog]

11. 博客：网络日志

真 the hugely popular blog 十分受欢迎的博客

扩 shut down sb's blog 关掉某人的博客

post a picture on the blog

在博客上发布一张图片

v. 写博客；写网络日志

真 carry on blogging 继续更新博客

扩 blog on a weekly basis 每周发布一次博客

1. 高中词(3词)

n. 路线；路途

真 travel a familiar route 走一条熟悉的路线  

扩 the route to the lab 去往实验室的路线  

a study of major bird migratory route  

一项关于鸟类迁徙主要路线的研究

astronaut $ ^{1} $ ★☆☆ [ˈæstrənɔɪt]

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ novelist [ˈnɒvəlɪst] n. 小说家

cart $ ^{1} $ ★☆☆ [kat]

###### n. 购物车；手推车

knock a supermarket cart aside 把超市的购物车撞到一边

journalism' ★☆☆ [ˈdʒɜːnəlɪzəm]

scan $ ^{1} $ ★☆☆ [skæn]

# 第五章 写作表达积累

### 第一单元 话题常用词汇

## 第一节 社会生活(25词)

## 一、社会发展(16词)

#### society

[sə'saiəti]

###### n. 社会

搭 introduce policies that benefit society as a whole 推行造福全社会的政策

Advances in digital technology are deeply influencing modern society.

数字技术的发展正深刻影响着现代社会

联 social a. ①社会的(corrupt~morals 败坏社会风气); ②社交的(have an active~life 社交生活丰富; develop~skills 培养社交能力)

socially ad. 在社会上(~unacceptable behavior 社会上不被接受的行为; help children from~disadvantaged families 帮助来自社会弱势家庭的儿童)

community n. 社会(The international~must work together to deal with global challenges.国际社会必须通力合作以应对全球性的挑战.)

#### urban

[ˈɜːbən]

###### a. 城市的

搭 a sharp rise/increase in urban population  

城市人口的激增  

migrate from rural to urban areas in search of work 为了找工作从农村移居到城市  

Young people prefer urban living despite its rising cost. 尽管成本在不断上升，年轻人仍青睐城市生活。

派 urbanization n. 城市化（challenges caused by rapid~快速城市化带来的挑战）

联 city n. 城市

(enjoy exploring a~享受探索城市的乐趣)

反 rural a. 乡村的

(support~education 支持乡村教育)

### economy [ɪˈkɒnəmi]

###### n. 经济

Thanks to China's stable/booming economy, the development of China is expected to be expected to be得益于中国稳定/繁荣的经济 development policies to stimulate domestic economy. It is expected to be expected to be in the development of China's economic and economic development.

#### development [dr'veləmpənt]

###### n. 发展

place a high value on innovation-driven development 非常重视创新驱动发展

promote the development of creative thinking skills 促进创新思维能力的发展

Schools should encourage the full development of a student's talents.

学校应鼓励学生全面发展才能。

联 growth n. 增长；发展（a huge~area/industry 一个高速发展的领域/行业）

progress n. 进步（make remarkable~in fighting poverty 在抗击贫困上取得显著进展）

advance n. 发展；进步（rapid~in science and technology 科技的迅猛发展）

#### gap

[gæp]

###### n. 差距；隔阂

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ an activity that helps narrow the culture/ cultural gap 有助于缩小文化差异的活动

The gap between (the) rich and (the) poor is still widening.贫富差距仍在拉大。

Mutual understanding is the key to closing/bridging the generation gap.

相互理解是消除代沟的关键。

#### technology

[tek'nɒlədʒi]

#### 11. 技术；科技

搭 apply digital technology to the classroom

将数字技术应用于课堂

invest heavily in energy-saving technology

大力投资节能技术

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ technological a. 技术的 (an era of rapid ~ change 技术变革迅猛的时代)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ technical a. 技术的( provide students with~ training 为学生提供技术培训)

#### Internet

['intənet]

###### n. 互联网

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ on the Internet 在网上

be addicted to the Internet 沉迷网络

联 online a. 在线的 (Online learning has been on the rise. 在线学习呈上升趋势。)

addiction n. 瘾(smartphone/social media~智能手机/社交媒体成瘾)

#### digital

[ˈdɪdʒɪtl]

###### a. 数字(化)的

 $ \underline{\text{搔}} $ keep abreast of the digital revolution

紧跟数字化革命的步伐

close/narrow/bridge the digital gap/divide

缩小/弥合数字鸿沟

### virtual [ 'vɜːtʃuəl ]

###### a. 虚拟的

搭 take a virtual tour of a campus/museum 对校园/博物馆进行虚拟游览 be immersed in a virtual world/community 沉浸于虚拟世界/社区

#### environment [In'vaɪrənmənt]

###### n.<the ~>自然环境；生态环境

措施 avoid polluting the environment

避免污染自然环境

measures to protect/preserve the environment

保护自然环境的措施

☑ environmental a. 自然环境的(raise~awareness among the public 提升公众的环保意识) environmentally ad. 在环境方面(develop~friendly products 开发环保产品)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ ecological a. 生态的( harm/upset the~balance of an area 破坏某地区的生态平衡) ecosystem n. 生态系统( disrupt the delicate/fragile~破坏脆弱的生态系统)

### pollution [pəˈluːʃn]

###### n. 污染

control air/water/environmental pollution

治理空气/水/环境污染

cut/reduce plastic/chemical/industrial pollution

减少塑料/化学/工业污染

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ pollute v. 污染(~ the air/water supply/environment 污染空气/供水/环境)

pollutant n. 污染物(cut/reduce emissions of ~s 减少污染物的排放)

#### resource [ri'sɔːs]

###### n. 资源

a great way to utilize renewable resources

一种利用可再生资源的好方法

save/conserve water/energy/marine resources

节约水资源/能源/海洋资源

promote sustainable exploitation of natural

resources 推动自然资源的可持续开发

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ energy n.能源(save/conserve~节能；green/renewable~绿色/可再生能源)

recycle v.回收利用(~waste paper/plastic bottles回收废纸/塑料瓶)

wildlife n.野生动植物(protect native/endangered~保护本土/濒危野生物种)

extinction n. 灭绝 (save endangered species from ~ 拯救濒危物种以防灭绝)

##### balance

[ˈbæls]

###### n. 平衡；均衡

Maintain the fragile ecological balance

维持脆弱的生态平衡

Keep a balance between tradition and modernity

兼顾传统和现代

1. 同等重视；使平衡

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ balance work and personal interests

兼顾工作与个人兴趣

balance career and home/family life

兼顾事业与家庭生活

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ balanced a.平衡的

(stick to a~diet/meal 坚持均衡饮食)

[ˈkʌltʃə(r)]

##### culture

#### 11. 文化

搭 meet people from different cultures

结识不同文化背景的人

suffer from/overcome (a) culture shock

遭受/克服文化冲击

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ cultural a. 文化的 (protect/preserve our ~ heritages 保护我们的文化遗产)

##### tradition

###### n. 传统

[trəˈdɪʃn]

择 keep old/ancient artistic traditions alive 将古老的艺术传统延续下去 cherish China's unique cultural traditions 珍惜中国独特的文化传统

派 traditional a. 传统的

(preserve~values 维护传统价值观)

☑ custom n. 习俗 (respect and preserve local ~s 尊重并保护地方风俗)

#### exchange [iks'tʃeɪndʒ]

###### n. 交换；交流

expand/broaden academic/cultural exchanges 拓展学术/文化交流

have an exchange of ideas with senior professionals 与资深专家交流想法

##### V. 交换；交流

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ exchange ideas/views with leading scholars 与顶尖学者交流想法/意见

## 二、个人生活(9词)

life [laɪf]

###### n. ①生活经历

搭 the rapid pace of modern life 现代生活的快节奏

Never let your work dominate your life.

永远不要让工作支配你的生活。

②(某种方式的)生活

搭 pursue a better/higher quality of life  

追求更高质量的生活  

live/lead a full/meaningful/colorful life  

过充实/有意义/多彩的生活

##### interest

[ˈɪntrəst]

###### n. ①兴趣；关注

搭 have a deep interest in outdoor activities

interesting a.有趣的(make classes more~for students 使课堂对学生而言更有趣)  

②业余爱好

搭 develop/explore leisure interests 发展/探索业余爱好 pursue one's varied/diverse interests 追求自己多种多样的爱好

联 hobby n. 业余爱好 (find time to pursue one's hobbies 找时间发展自己的业余爱好)

#### health

[helθ]

###### n. 健康

maintain one's physical and mental health 保持自己的身心健康 present a potential threat to public health 对公众健康构成潜在威胁 We should try not to risk our own health. 我们应该尽量不拿自己的健康冒险。

联 fit a. 健康的 (take regular exercise to keep/stay~经常锻炼以保持健康)

fitness n. 健康 (maintain~保持健康; sign up for~courses 报名参加健身课程)

###### n. 期望；指望

##### burden

[ˈbɜːdn]

###### n.（义务、责任等的）重担，负担

#### family

[ˈfæməli]

###### n. 家，家庭（包括父母子女）

反 hate n. 憎恨

(remove/delete~speech 删除仇恨言论)

hatred n.仇恨(have a deep~of/for waste of resources 对资源浪费深恶痛绝)

[keə(r)]

###### n. 照顾；关怀

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ share housework and the care of children分担家务和照看小孩的工作

take tender care of pets/animals/plants

悉心照料宠物/动物/植物

provide necessary care for patients/the elderly

为病人/老人提供必要的护理

派 caring a. 关心他人的(provide a~environment 提供一个充满关怀的环境)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ care for/look after 照料(~the sick, elderly and disabled 关心老弱病残)

#### promise [ˈprɒmɪs]

#### 11. 诺言：承诺

措施 keep promises given to our friends/other people 信守向朋友/他人许下的承诺

Businesses should be punished for breaking their promise of product quality.

违背产品质量承诺的商家应受到处罚。

##### 承诺：许诺

 $ \underline{\text{揩}} $ promise not to violate professional ethics承诺不会违反职业道德

#### sincere [sin'sɪə(r)]

###### a. 诚挚的；真诚的

Please accept our sincere thanks/apologies.

请接受我们诚挚的谢意/歉意

make/offer a sincere apology to you for my fault 因我的过失向您真诚致歉

make sincere efforts to build a harmonious relationship 真诚地努力建立融洽关系

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ sincerely ad.诚挚地；由衷地( be~grateful for your help 由衷感谢您的帮助)

 $ \underline{联} $ honest/truthful a. 诚实的(learn to be~about our feelings 学会坦诚表达感受)

#### respect [ri'spekt]

###### n./v. 尊敬；尊重

播 treat our parents/friends/elders with respect  

尊重我们的父母/朋友/长辈  

respect other people's opinions/privacy/  

lifestyles 尊重他人的意见/隐私/生活方式  

respect laws/social norms/rules and regulations  

遵守法律/社会规范/规章制度

 $ \overrightarrow{派} $ respectful a. 表示尊敬的

(be~of other cultures 尊重其他文化)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ esteem n. 尊重(public~for doctors/teachers 大众对医生/教师的尊重)

self-esteem n. 自尊 (build/boost/improve students'~培养/提升学生的自尊)

##### understand

[Andə'stænd]

#### 1. 理解；体谅

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ understand how other people feel

理解他人的感受

understand what others have been through

同情他人的遭遇

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ understanding n.理解

( promote mutual ~ between teachers and students/parents and children/doctors and patients 促进师生/亲子/医患之间的相互理解)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ forgiving a.宽容的( be~ of other people's difficulties 体谅他人的难处)

generous a. 宽宏大量的( be~ enough to overlook other people's little mistakes 大度地不计较他人的小过失)

##### trust

[trast]

###### n./v. 信任；信赖

搭 try not to betray our close friends' trust

尽量不要辜负密友的信任

trust in our own abilities to meet the

challenge of job seeking

相信自己有能力应对求职的挑战

派 trusting a. 轻信的(avoid being too~of other people 避免过于轻信他人)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ faith n. 信任

( keep~with our friends 对朋友守信用)

#### integrity

[In'tegrati]

###### n. 诚实；正直

搭 be a person of the highest integrity

做光明磊落的人

protect/preserve/safeguard/defend academic

integrity 维护/捍卫学术诚信

principle [ˈprɪnsəpl]

###### n. 道德原则；行为准则

搭 adhere to the principles of sustainable development 坚持可持续发展的原则

teach children to obey/follow/observe moral principles 教导孩子遵守道德准则

stick to the principle that everyone should be treated equally 坚持一视同仁的原则

#### modest

[ˈmɒdɪst]

###### a. 谦虚的；谦逊的

搭 be modest about our success/achievements 不夸耀自己的成就

be modest about our role in group work 不夸耀自己在小组工作中的作用

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ modesty n. 谦虚 (show ~ when receiving a compliment 受到称赞时表现出谦虚)

 $ \underline{联} $ humble a.虚心的( be~enough to learn from our mistakes 从错误中虚心学习)

humility n.谦逊 ( have the ~ to admit/acknowledge our mistakes 虚心承认错误)

#### rational

[ˈræʃnəl]

###### a. 理性的；合理的

Keep calm and rational in the face of unexpected changes and challenges 面对出乎意料的变化和挑战时保持冷静和理性

派 rationally ad. 理智地

(act/think~基于理性行动/思考)

rationality n.理性

 $ \underline{联} $ sensible a. 明智的( make a~choice/decision 做出明智的选择/决定)

反 irrational a. 不理智的 (avoid ~ consumer behavior 避免不理性的消费行为)

#### patience

[ˈpeɪʃns]

###### n. 耐心；忍耐力

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ do not lose patience when there is poor communication 沟通不畅时不要失去耐心

联 patient a. 有耐心的 (be ~ with kids/slow learners 对小孩/学得慢的学生有耐心)

 $ \underline{反} $ impatience n. 不耐烦( try to curb/control/ contain our~尽力克制自己的急躁情绪)

## 二、个人发展(14词)

#### attitude

[ˈæˌtɪtjuːd]

#### 11. 态度；看法

Being competitive is an attitude of mind.

好竞争是一种心态。

take/adopt a responsible attitude to work

对工作采取负责任的态度

keep/maintain a positive attitude towards life

对生活保持积极的态度

#### curiosity

[ kjuəri'vsəti]

###### n. 好奇心

 $ \underline{\text{搔}} $ intellectual curiosity 求知欲

satisfy one's curiosity 满足好奇心

arouse/excite one's curiosity 激起好奇心

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ curious a. 好奇的( be/feel~ about the world around us 对周遭世界感到好奇)

#### far-sighted

[ˌfɑːˈsaɪtɪd]

###### a. 有远见的；深谋远虑的

搭 develop far-sighted plans for our future

为自己的未来制定有远见的规划

make far-sighted decisions about what to do

after college

对大学毕业后的安排做出有远见的决策

 $ \underline{\text{反}} $ short-sighted a.目光短浅的

( avoid~thinking 避免短视思维)

#### vision

[ˈvɪʒn]

###### n. 眼光；远见

搭 develop a wide/broad vision

培养广阔的视野

have a clear vision of our goals

对自己的目标有清晰的展望

avoid a narrow vision of the future/our life

避免狭隘地展望未来/人生

#### horizon

[həˈraɪzn]

###### n. 眼界；阅历

 $ \underline{\text{揩}} $ widen/broaden our horizons 开阔眼界 expand intellectual horizons 拓宽知识面 avoid limiting our horizons to what is within our comfort zone 避免将我们的眼界局限于自己的舒适区之内

### opportunity

[đọp tjuːnəti]

###### n. 机会；时机

Career opportunities 职业机会

take this opportunity to thank you for your support 借此机会感谢您的支持

take every opportunity to expand our work experience 利用一切机会拓展工作经验

seize/grasp precious opportunities to enhance our competitiveness

抓住提升自身竞争力的宝贵机会

#####  $ \underline{联} $ chance n.机会

（注：搭配方式与 opportunity 基本一致）

#### achieve

[əˈtʃiːv]

##### V.（尤指经过努力）达到，实现

搭 achieve success/progress through hard work  

通过努力取得成功/进步  

achieve good exam results by studying hard  

通过努力学习取得优异的考试成绩  

try our best to achieve our goals/dreams/ambitions 竭尽全力实现目标/梦想/抱负

派 achievement n. 成就

(Success should not be measured only by educational~s. 成功不应仅由学业成绩来衡量)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ attain/accomplish v. 实现

(注:搭配方式与 achieve 基本一致)

#### habit

[ˈhæbɪt]

###### N. 习惯

 $ \underline{\text{播}} $ form/develop good study/personal habits

养成良好的学习/个人习惯

kick/break the habit of waiting until the last

minute to start 改掉不到最后一刻不动手的习惯

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ habitual a.习惯性的

(never become a liar 永远不要撒谎成性)

#### challenge

[ˈtʃælɪndʒ]

###### n. 挑战

搭 turn a challenge into an opportunity

化挑战为机遇

enjoy the challenge of trying something new

享受尝试新事物的挑战

face up to/confront tough challenges in our life

直面人生的艰巨挑战

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ challenging a.有挑战性的

(take~work 承担有挑战性的工作)

#### overcome

[đầuđắk]

#### 1. 克服；战胜

overcome hardships/barriers/obstacles

克服困难/阻碍

overcome challenges/adversities/setbacks

克服挑战/逆境/挫折

#### goal

[gəul]

###### n. 目标；目的

 $ \underline{\text{擂}} $ set ourselves attainable personal goals

为自己设定可实现的个人目标

establish ourselves clear life/career goals

为自己设定明确的人生/事业目标

fight hard for achieving/realizing ambitious

goals 为实现远大目标而努力奋斗

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ aim/target/objective n.目标

(注:搭配方式与 goal 基本一致)

#### ambition

[æm'bɪʃn]

###### n. 志向；抱负

strive hard for our life-long ambitions

为实现终生追求的目标而奋发图强

have an ambition to pursue a teaching career

有志于从事教育职业

harbor/entertain an ambition to achieve

career success 有志于成就一番事业

 $ \underline{\text{派}} $ ambitious a. 有雄心的

(Parents are~for their children.父母对孩子期望很高。)

 $ \underline{联} $ aspiration n. 志向

(have no~for fame and fortune 不求名利)

#### comfort zone

### 舒适区（使人感到舒适、放松或在其掌控之下的状态）

Stay within/leave/expand our comfort zone  

待在/离开/拓展自己的舒适区  

go/get/step/move/break out of/outside our comfort zone 走出自己的舒适区  

push ourselves out of/outside/beyond our comfort zone 逼自己走出舒适区

#### friendship

[ˈfrendʃɪp]

###### n. 友谊；朋友关系

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ cherish friendships formed in our student days 珍惜学生时代建立的友谊

avoid doing things that ruin/destroy friendships 避免做破坏友谊的事

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ friendly a. 友好的( be~to the people around us 友善对待我们身边的人)

relationship n. 关系( develop a harmonious family~培养融洽的家庭关系)

### 第二单元 框架搭建词汇

## 一、应用

##### 邀请：invite · invitation · attend · attach

##### invite

[ɪnˈvaɪt]

V. 邀请

cordially/warmly/sincerely invite you to

(attend) the reading seminar

热诚/热情/真诚地邀请您参加阅读研讨会

invitation [ˌɪnvɪˈteɪʃn]

1. 邀请

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ receive/accept/decline an invitation 收到/接受/婉拒邀请

extend to you an invitation to attend the contest as a judge 邀请您担任比赛评委

attend

[ə'tend]

v. 出席；参加 = participate in/join

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ attend a lecture/conference/seminar 参加讲座/会议/研讨会

attach

「əˈtætʃ」

v. 把……附上=enclose

 $ \underline{搭} $ My resume is attached.随函附上我的简历

#### 2 建议：suggestion · tip

#### suggestion

[sə'dzestfan]

n. 建议；提议 = advice（多指专业人士的建议）

take your suggestions into serious account  

认真考虑您的建议  

offer suggestions on how to relieve anxiety  

提出关于如何缓解焦虑的建议

[tup]

tip

n. 指点；实用的提示

 travel/cooking/safety tips

旅行小贴士/烹饪小诀窍/安全忠告

give you some tips on/for improving English

给你一些提高英语的小窍门

3 推荐：recommend · impress · glimpse

recommend [rekə'mend]

V. 推荐：举荐

搭 recommend sb for the post

推荐某人任职这一岗位

(highly/strongly) recommend this app to you

(极力)向你推荐这个应用程序

impress [im'pres]

##### v. 给……留下好印象；使钦佩

搭 it impresses sb that.../sb is impressed that...

令某人印象深刻的是……

I am impressed by the originality of the

candidate's suggestion. 候选者所提建议的独

创性令我印象深刻

#### glimpse

[ glimps ]

###### n. 短暂的感受（或体验、领会）

give/offer you a quick glimpse into China's history and culture

使您快速了解中国历史和文化

Science courses give us a glimpse of the time-tested scientific method. 理科课程能让我们对久经检验而行之有效的科学方法有初步的认识。

##### notice

noutis

###### n. 通知；启事 = announcement

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ Please pay close attention to this notice. 请密切关注此通知

##### inform

in'fo:m]

##### v. 知会; 通知 = notify

Please inform us about/of your decision.

请告知我们您的决定..

recruit [ri'kruːt]

V. 招募

搭 recruit new talents 招募新人才

recruit new members to the club 社团纳新

recruit international students to teach English

招募留学生教英语

#### submit

[səb'mɪt]

##### v. 提交；呈递

 $ \underline{\text{tng}} $ submit the speech draft 提交演讲稿 submit my resignation 提交我的辞呈 submit a(n) application form/entry form/proposal 提交申请表/报名表/提案

#### sign up for

报名参加=register for

sign up for a(n) course/exam

报名参加一门课程/考试

##### 介绍：organize · event · schedule · theme · feature · look forward to · contact

c:genaiz]

v. 组织；筹备 = hold

搭 organize a book donation program  

组织图书捐赠活动

event

[i'vent]

###### n. 公开活动；（体育运动的）比赛项目

搭 the upcoming campus/sporting events  

即将到来的校园/体育活动

[ˈskedʒuːl]

###### n. 日程安排 v. 为……安排时间

搭 on schedule 按预定时间

ahead of/behind schedule 先于/迟于预定时间

The meeting is scheduled to commence on Monday. 会议定于周一举行。

#### theme

[θizm]

###### n. 主题

搭 a lecture on the theme of waste recycling 以垃圾回收为主题的讲座

On the theme of Chinese culture, this meeting is designed to (do)...

本次会议以中国文化为主题，旨在……

##### feature

「｀ｈｉｔｓｄ（ｒ）」

##### v. 以……为特色；由……主演

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ a film that features an all-star cast

由全明星阵容主演的电影

an exhibition featuring traditional crafts

重点展出传统手工艺品的展览

#### look forward to

##### （高兴地）盼望，期待

 $ \underline{搭} $ I look forward to seeing you at the event. 期待在活动现场见到您.

#### contact

[ˈkɒntækt]

##### v./n. 联系；联络

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ stay/keep in (close) contact with friends 与朋友保持(密切)联系 a chance to come into contact with famous figures 与名人接触的机会

#### 6 申请：apply · candidate · qualification

#### apply

[əˈplaɪ]

##### V.（通常以书面形式）申请

控 apply for a job/scholarship/student loan

申请工作/奖学金/助学贷款

apply for admission to a university/apply to a university 申请入读大学

#### candidate

[ˈkændɪdət]

n. 候选人；申请人

 $ \underline{搭} $ As a competitive candidate for this position,

my key strengths are... 作为此职位有竞争力的候选人，我的主要优势是……

#### qualification

[ˌkwɒlɪfɪˈkeɪʃn]

###### n. 资格；学历

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ vocational qualifications 职业资历 have the qualifications for this job 具备胜任这项工作的资格

I am convinced that my qualifications could be a suitable match for your requirements. 我坚信自己的条件能契合你们的要求。

#### 7 辞职：quit · resign · position

#### quit

[kwit]

v. 离开(工作职位、学校等) = leave

 $ \underline{\text{擡}} $ quit/leave a club 退出社团

quit/leave my job 辞去自己的职务

resign

[ri'zain]

##### v. 辞职

resign my job/post/position 辞去自己的工作/职务

#### position

#### [u]sɪz'ed

###### n. 职位；职务=post

腾 available positions 空缺的工作职位

be not equal to/competent for the current position 无法胜任目前的岗位

the professional knowledge required for the position 该职位所需的专业知识

I am confident enough to be a strong candidate for this position.我有足够的信心成为该职位的有力候选人。

#### 8 道歉：apology · make up for

#### apology

[ˈeɪpədʒiːl]

###### n. 道歉；认错

搭 offer/express my deep apologies for...

因……深表歉意

( = be sorry for.../apologize for...)

#### make up for

##### 弥补；补偿 = compensate for

搭 To make up for my fault, I will submit the completed thesis... 为了弥补我的过错，我将提交完整的论文……

#### 咨询：inquire · inquiry · reply

#### inquire

[ɪnˈkwɑɪə(r)]

##### v. 询问；打听（英式拼写为 enquire）

I am writing to inquire about your job advertisement online. 我写信是想咨询一下你们刊登在网上的招聘广告

May I kindly inquire if you would be so kind as to lend me help in finding opportunities to gain experience in teaching mathematics?

我想请问您是否能帮我找一找积累数学教学经验的机会？

#### inquiry

in kwari

n. 询问；打听（英式拼写为 enquiry）

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ make an inquiry 咨询

answer an inquiry 回复咨询

#### reply

[ru'plaɪ]

#### 17. 答复

 $ \underline{\text{搔}} $ look forward to your early/prompt reply 期待您的早日回复

#### 10 感谢：appreciate · grateful · gratitude

#### appreciate

əˈpriːʃieɪt]

v. 感谢 = thank sb for (doing) sth

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ Your presence will be greatly appreciated.

我们将非常感谢您的出席

#### grateful

`greitfl`

###### a. 感激的

 $ \underline{搔} $ be grateful to all the teachers for their help 感谢所有老师的帮助

#### gratitude

[ˈɡrætjuːd]

#### 11. 感激之情

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ express my deep gratitude ( to you ) for all you did 向您所做的一切深表感激

Please accept the gift as a token of my gratitude.请收下这份表示谢意的礼物

In gratitude for your assistance, we will provide free accommodation and meals during the project.我们将在项目期间提供免费的食宿，以感谢你的协助

## 二、描述

##### 描述图画内容：depict · present · scene

#### depict

di'pikt]

v. 描绘 = describe/portray

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ as (is) depicted in the picture 如图所示

#### present

[pri'zent]

v. 展现；表现 = display

搭 the picture presents a situation where.../a young man who...图片展示了一幅……的场景/一位……的年轻人

##### scene

sin]

###### n. 场面；情景

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ a familiar scene on campus

熟悉的校园场景

display a scene of harmony where...

展示了一幅和谐的场景，其中……

a(n) comic/ironic/joyful/touching/shocking/regrettable/encouraging scene 一幅有趣/讽刺/令人欣喜/令人感动/令人震惊/令人遗憾/鼓舞人心的场景

#### 2 描述图画特点：vivid · thought-provoking · distinct

vivid

 $ ^{1} $vivid

###### a. 清晰的；生动的

撂 the picture is a vivid depiction of...

图片生动地描绘了……

thought-provoking 'θὺt practøukῃη]

###### a. 发人深省的

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ a thought-provoking question/article 发人深省的问题/文章

The picture conveys a straightforward but thought-provoking message.图画传达的信息简单却引人深思。

This statement is quite thought-provoking, and I go along with it. 这一论点颇为发人深省，我对此表示赞同。

##### distinct

[di'stɪŋkt]

###### a. 截然不同的；有区别的 = contrasting

搭 as distinct from the former 与前者完全不同 two distinct ways of.../attitudes towards... 两种截然不同的……方式/态度

##### 描述图画主体：symbolize · manner

##### symbolize

simbélaiz

v. 象征；代表=represent/stand for/be a symbol of

搭 Light symbolizes life and hope.

光明象征着生命和希望.

A “clock track” symbolizes college journey.

“时钟轨道”象征着大学旅程

##### manner

[ˈmænə(r)]

###### n. 态度；举止

搭 have a relaxed/confident/calm manner  

态度悠闲/自信/从容  

in a rash/professional/distracted manner  

轻率/专业/心不在焉地

#### 4 描述图画内涵：caption · reveal · reflect · illustrate · reminder · criticism

#### caption

[ˈkæpʃn]

v. 给(图片、漫画等)加文字说明 n. 文字说明

 $ \underline{\text{擋}} $ the drawing is captioned "..."

图片注有文字说明"……"

the caption conveys the core message:...

图中文字传达出核心信息：……

[r'viːl]

##### v. 揭示；显示

搭 The phenomenon revealed in the picture is not rare nowadays.

图中揭示的现象如今并不少见

reflect ri'flekt

v. 反映；表明 = mirror

摇 reflect a common social phenomenon/a noteworthy trend that... 反映了一种普遍的社会现象/一种值得注意的趋势，即……

##### illustrate

['læstreit]

##### v.（用示例、图画等）说明，解释=show

 $ \underline{\text{搪}} $ illustrate the importance/significance of teamwork 说明合作的重要性

#### reminder

[ri'mainde(r)]

###### n. 提醒人的事物

搭 provide a constant reminder of the fragility of life 时刻提醒人们生命的脆弱

##### criticism

[ 'kritiszəm]

###### n. 批评；批判

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ accept criticism 接受批评

draw/attract/provoke criticism 引起批评

#### 5 描述普遍现象：common · widespread · popular

common

[ˈkɒmən]

a. 常见的；普遍的 = commonplace

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ common sense 常识

it is common knowledge that...

人们普遍认为……

It is common (place) for young adults to stay up late. 年轻人熬夜很常见

it is common for us to hear about the cases where...我们常听说……的情况

#### widespread

[ˈwaɪdspred]

###### a. 普遍的；广泛的

搭 the widespread use/availability of technology 技术的广泛使用/普及

there is/are widespread concern/fears/belief that...人们普遍担心/认为……

#### popular

['pɒpjələ(r)]

###### a. 普遍的；流行的 = prevalent

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ a popular belief/opinion/view/idea

普遍的观念

recently become popular among consumers

近来受到消费者的青睐

##### 描述背景特点：age · era · time

age

[eɪdʒ]

###### n.（尤指文明或技术发展的）时代，时期

搭 the industrial/information age 工业/信息时代 the age of big data/artificial intelligence (AI) 大数据/人工智能时代

era

[ˈɪərə]

n.（以某些特殊事件为标志的）时代，年代

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ an era of entertainment/knowledge explosion

娱乐/知识爆炸的时代

enter/usher in an era of instant communication

进入即时通讯的时代

##### time

[taim]

###### n. 时期；时代

搭配 keep pace with the times 跟上时代

be out of step with/fall behind the times

跟不上时代

in a time of constant change/stiff competition/uncertainty 在一个瞬息万变/竞争激烈/充满不确定性的时代

##### 描述问题/困扰：problem · issue · concern · worry

#### problem

[ˈprɒbləm]

##### issue

[ˈɪʃuː]

##### concern

[ kənˈsɜːn ]

[dt'bent]

trend]

klem]

##### 陈述结果：result · consequence · impact · influence · lead · end up (in/with/doing sth)

 $  \text{rt}^{\prime}z\text{alt}  $

[ˈkɒnsɪkwəns]

thus/therefore/so that,后接句子)

reind3

[nəb]

#### （谚语、歌词、故事等）内容是

#### put

##### v. 说；表达

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ as sb put(s) it 如某人所说

(注:谓语时态用现在时或过去时均可)

#### according to

According to a recent report/study, 根据最近的一项报道/研究

逻辑衔接词：moreover · though · despite · however · instead · while · meanwhile · by/in contrast · likewise · thus · in other words · in brief

##### moreover

[ mɔːrˈəʊvə(r) ]

##### ad. 此外（体现补充/递进关系）

 $ \underline{\text{例}} $  $ \underline{\text{Moreover}} $，a variety of talent recruitment websites，including those specially designed for foreigners in China，are viable options.  $ \underline{\text{其次}} $，各种人才招聘网站，包括专门为在华外国人设计的网站，都是可行的选择。

联 furthermore; besides: in addition; additionally; what is more; on top of that(均可用于补充信息，相较而言 besides 不够正式) for one thing...for another... (主要用于列举原因)

#### though

[đọa]

conj. 虽然；(用于主句后引出补充说明) 不过(体现让步/转折关系)

例 ①Some people, fewer books  $ \underline{\text{though}} $ they have, do everything possible to read them.有些人 $ \underline{\text{虽然}} $藏书不多,却想方设法为自己创造读书的机会

②A better approach is to lay out a detailed career plan in advance,  $ \underline{\text{though}} $ it is hard for most soon-to-be graduates.更好的办法是提前制定详细的职业规划, $ \underline{\text{不过}} $这对大多数即将毕业的学生来说有些困难。

 $ \underline{联} $ although(虽然/即使；不过/然而) even though/if(虽然；即使)

#### despite [dr'spait]

##### prep. 即使；尽管（体现让步关系）

例 We should adopt a positive outlook on life  $ \underline{\text{despite}} $ its inevitable twists and turns.  $ \underline{\text{尽管}} $人生难免会有挫折,我们也应该抱有积极的态度

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ in spite of(+照应上文内容的代词、名词或名词结构)

hạo evê(r)]

##### ad. 然而；不过（体现转折关系）

例  $ \underline{\text{However}} $，the otherwise wonderful scene is overshadowed by something extremely unpleasant.  $ \underline{\text{然而}} $，一种极其糟糕的情形破坏了这本该美好的场景.

联 but; yet; still; nevertheless; nonetheless (but 和 yet 是连词，其余为副词)

actually; in fact; as a matter of fact(也可表示转折，常用于反映理论或理想与现实之间的差异)

#### instead

[In'sted]

##### ad. 反而，却；代替，而不是（体现转折关系）

例 ① Many shortsighted students dismiss those challenging courses as burdensome and take much easier classes  $ \underline{\text{instead}} $.许多目光短浅的学生把富有挑战性的课程视为一种负担，将其排除在考虑范围之外， $ \underline{\text{而}} $去上更容易的课。

②  $ \underline{\text{Instead of}} $ giving in to the pressure to follow the herd, we should be courageous to stick to what we feel enthusiastic about.我们不能屈服于从众的压力，而应敢于坚持自己热衷的事物。

 $ \underline{联} $ rather than 例: What is needed is a sustained effort to conquer difficulties  $ \underline{\text{rather than}} $ an excuse to give up.我们需要通过不懈努力克服困难，而非找借口放弃。

while [wail]

conj.（用于句首）尽管；（对比两件事物）而（体现让步/转折/对比关系）

例 ① $ \underline{While} $ we may not yet have reached the point of no return, much evidence has warned us we may be getting awfully close.  $ \underline{\text{尽管}} $事态还未到“不可挽救”的地步,但大量证据已经警示我们可能离此地步相当近了。

② In the left picture, the father keeps instructing his son to concentrate on his study  $ \underline{\text{while}} $ he himself is having fun watching TV. 左图中,父亲一直吩咐儿子专心学习,  $ \underline{\text{而}} $他自己却在开心地看电视。

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ whereas conj.然而,尽管

(用以比较或对比两个事实)

meanwhile [ˈmiːnwaɪl]

##### ad. 与此同时；对比之下

##### （体现时间/对比关系）

 $ \underline{\text{例}} $ ①A pathetic old man has just been kicked away by his eldest son.  $ \underline{\text{Meanwhile}} $，his other three children are defending their own goal watchfully lest he enter it.一位可怜的老人刚被自己的大儿子踢出门外。 $ \underline{\text{与此同时}} $，其他三个子女正严守各自的“球门”，谨防他进入。

② The student on the left dismisses the lecture as nearly worthless. The student on the right,  $ \underline{\text{meanwhile}} $，views it in a positive light.左侧的学生认为讲座几乎无用。 $ \underline{\text{与之相比}} $，右侧的学生则从积极的角度看待这场讲座。

 $ \underline{联} $ in the meanwhile/meantime 与此同时 at the same time 与此同时；不过

#### by/in contrast

##### 相比之下（体现对比关系）

 $ \underline{\text{例}} $  $ \underline{\text{By/In contrast}} $，the boy in the right picture is reclining in a comfortable armchair with no intention of doing his homework.  $ \underline{\text{相比之下}} $，右图中的男生倚靠在舒适的扶椅上，丝毫不打算做功课。

注：by contrast 和 in contrast 均可用在句首和句中，后者常用于 in contrast to/with... (与……形成对比) 这一结构中。

 $ \underline{擂} $ by/in marked/sharp/stark/striking contrast

形成鲜明对比

 $ \underline{联} $ compared with/to sth 与某物相比

unlike/different from sth 与某物不同

on the contrary 与之相反

on (the) one hand...on the other hand

一方面……另一方面……(引出不同的观点)

#### likewise

[ˈlaɪkwɑɪz]

##### ad. 同样地，类似地；也（体现相似关系）

例 In the picture, the attacker imagines the goalkeeper as a giant.  $ \underline{\text{Likewise}} $, the goalkeeper thinks of himself as a dwarf.图中,进攻球员把守门员想象成了巨人。 $ \underline{\text{无独有偶}} $,守门员把自己想成了小矮人。

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ similarly; similar to sth; in the same way(均可表示相似关系)

[∂ $ \Lambda $s]

##### ad. 因此，从而；这样，如此（体现因果关系）

例 ① It is  $ \underline{thus} $ totally unnecessary for us to hesitate to do what we enjoy for fear of disapproval from others.因此，我们完全没必要因担心他人的反对而不去做自己喜欢的事。

② An optimistic attitude allows us to keep composure in the face of obstacles,  $ \underline{thus} $ enabling us to put all our energies into navigating them.乐观的心态能让我们镇定自若地面对阻碍， $ \underline{从而} $使我们能够将所有的精力用于寻找应对办法。

③ Chinese people become increasingly proud of their own national identity,  $ \underline{thus} $ leading to the rise in the public's preference for domestic products over recent years.中国人越来越为自己的民族身份感到自豪， $ \underline{从而} $使得近年来公众对国产品牌的偏好上升。

联 therefore; consequently; hence(用于句中时引出名词，如...hence the need for sth……因此有必要做某事)；so(连词)；so that(后接句子)

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ therefore；consequently；hence(用于句中时引出名词，如...hence the need for sth……因此有必要做某事)；so(连词)；so that(后接句子)thereby(通常后接分词短语作结果状语)

#### in other words

##### 换言之：换句话说（体现解释关系）

 $ \underline{\text{例}} $  $ \underline{\text{In other words}} $，persistence is the key to success. $ \underline{\text{换言之}} $，持之以恒便是我们取得成功的关键.

 $ \underline{联} $ that is to say; to put it another way

##### in brief

##### 总之；简言之（体现总结关系）

例  $ \underline{\text{In brief}} $，we should place weight on the breadth as well as depth of knowledge.  $ \underline{\text{简而言之}} $，除了知识的深度，我们也应注重知识的广度。

 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ in short; (to put it) in a nutshell; to summarize; to sum up; in sum; in summary; to conclude; in conclusion; overall; all in all; on the whole; in general; generally speaking; by and large; taking everything into account; all things considered(均可用于总结,但 overall 及之后的表达存在语义差异,不能完全互换)

## 四、建议

1 提出建议：advisable · sensible · imperative · pros and cons

##### advisable

[ ad'vaizabl ]

###### a. 明智的；可取的 = desirable

搭 It is advisable for the public to have a clear understanding of online shopping.

对公众来说对网购有清晰的认识是明智的

##### sensible

[ˈsensəbl]

###### a. 明智的；合理的 = wise/rational

搭 it is sensible to do sth/the sensible thing is to do sth 做某事是明智的

a sensible idea/choice/suggestion

明智的主意/抉择/建议

#### imperative im'perativ

###### a. 重要紧急的

搭 It is imperative to act now before the problem gets really serious. 必须现在就采取行动，而不是等到问题变得难以收拾.

#### pros and cons

##### 利弊

搭 Online learning has both its pros and cons.

上网课既有利也有弊..

weigh (up)/consider the pros and cons of

studying abroad 权衡出国留学的利弊

☑ advantages and disadvantages/merits and demerits 利弊/优缺点 (weigh/consider the

~ of social media/digital technology 权衡社交媒体/数字技术的利弊）

#### 2 介绍措施：action · move · measure

##### action

[ˈækʃn]

###### n.行动；行为

搭 take action to resolve difficulties

采取行动以解决困难

put a(n) idea/plan into action

把想法/计划付诸实施

Measures should be taken to raise the public's awareness of ecological protection and to encourage them to start with small actions.

应该采取措施以提高公众的生态保护意识，并鼓励他们从小事做起

##### move

[muːv]

###### n. 行动；举措 = step

搭 make a move/take steps to combat misinformation

采取措施以打击虚假信息

##### measure

[ˈmeʒə(r)]

###### n. 措施；方法

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ take/adopt (tough/drastic) measures to curb campus violence

采取(严厉的)措施以遏制校园暴力

### 说明做法：realize · tackle · navigate · give priority to · lay/put/place stress/emphasis on · prepare for · equip with

##### realize

[ˈriːələt]

##### v. 认识到；意识到

realize the importance and urgency of protecting wildlife

认识到保护野生动物的重要性和紧迫性

Online sellers should realize that they are ruining their own reputation by adopting such a wrong approach.网络商家应该明白，采用这种错误的方式是在毁坏自己的名声。

##### tackle

[ˈtækl]

v. 应付，处理（难题或局面）= address/deal with/cope with

摽 tackle the problem of food waste/population aging/data privacy 解决食物浪费/人口老龄化/数据隐私的问题

#### navigate

[ˈnævɪɡeɪt]

##### V. 找到正确方法（对付困难复杂的情况）

navigate obstacles/complicated situations 应对阻碍/复杂情形

navigate (through) challenges in life

设法应对生活中的挑战

navigate a pathway through a series of

developmental stages 设法应对不同的发展/成长阶段

#### give priority to

##### 重视；优先考虑

搭 give top priority to studies/self-improvement  

优先考虑学习/自我提升  

give high/main/major priority to professional development 高度重视职业发展

联 lay/put/place a high priority on 高度重视 (~personal integrity 高度重视个人诚信)

#### lay/put/place stress/emphasis on

##### 强调：重视

place equal emphasis on school and family education 同等重视学校与家庭教育 lay heavy stress on improving problem-solving skills 特别重视提升解决问题的能力

☑ give/attach importance to 重视(~protecting biodiversity 注重保护生物多样性)

#### prepare for

##### 使为……做好准备

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ prepare ourselves for changes and challenges in life 使我们自己为(迎接)人生的变化与挑战做好准备

prepare college students well/adequately for a competitive job market 使大学生对竞争激烈的就业市场做好充分准备

联 ready a. 准备好的 (get~for life's uncertainties 对人生的不确定因素做好准备)

#### equip with

##### 使具备

 $ \underline{\text{搭配}} $ equip one's children with first-class education 使自己的孩子接受一流的教育

equip students with the skills necessary for a job 使学生具备必备的工作技能

equip undergraduates with a broader perspective on life 使本科生具备更广阔的人生视野

联 equip college students for demanding jobs

使大学生能胜任高要求的工作

##### 发出呼吁：keep/bear in mind · high/about time

##### 谨记

 $ \underline{\text{擂}} $ keep/bear in mind that there is no shortcut to success 牢记成功无捷径

We should keep in mind that teamwork has its advantages and make efforts to collaborate with others.我们应该谨记团队合作有其优势，并努力与他人合作。

#### high/about time

##### 该是……的时候了

搭 It is high/about time (that) we took action/ should take action.

是我们采取行动的时候了。（句子使用虚拟语气）

As far as I am concerned, it is about time to take measures to address this issue.

我认为是采取措施来解决这一问题的时候了

## 五、总结

#### 7 总结升华：conclusion · matter

## conclusion

[ kənˈkluːʒn ]

#### 11. 结论：推论

From the above discussion, we can draw/reach/come to/arrive at a conclusion that...从上述讨论中，我们可以得出结论……

jump to/leap to a conclusion 或 draw a rash conclusion 贸然下结论

##### matter

「'mætə(r)」

##### v. 要紧：事关紧要 = count

 $ \underline{搭} $ what matters/counts most is...

最重要的是……

Therefore, we should remember that a positive mindset matters a great deal.因此，我们应该谨记积极的心态十分重要。

##### 展望未来：predictably · hopefully

#### predictably

[prı'diktəbli]

##### ad. 可预料地

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ Predictably, it is no easy task to tackle this issue, so we must strain every nerve.

可以预见的是,解决这一问题并非易事,因此我们必须全力以赴.

#### hopefully

həopfali

ad. 有望；但愿（此用法正确性存在争议，但是很常用）

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ hopefully, we will...我们有望……

hopefully with/through concerted efforts

希望通过共同努力

### 第三单元 词句多样表达

## 第一节 词的多样化

一、词性变换

#### 1 动词↔名词

contribute [kənˈtrɪbjʊt] v. 贡献↔contribution [ˌkɒntrɪˈbjuːʃn] n. 贡献  $ \underline{\text{搭}} $  $ \underline{\text{contribute to}} $ ↔make contributions to my hometown/rural revitalization 为我的家乡/乡村振兴 $ \underline{\text{做出贡献}} $

tend [tend] v. 往往会  $ \leftrightarrow $ tendency [ˈtendənsi] n. 倾向；偏好
 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $  $ \underline{\text{tend to}} $  $ \rightarrow $ have a tendency to shy away from normal social interactions  $ \underline{\text{往往会}} $ 回避正常的社交

decide [dɪˈsaɪd] v.决定→decision [dɪˈsɪʒn] n.决定
搭  $ \underline{\text{decide to→make/take a decision to}} $ work as an intern  $ \underline{\text{决定}} $实习
reach/come to/arrive at a decision on/about sth 就某事做出决定
a conscious/deliberate/hasty decision 慎重/深思熟虑/仓促的决定

choose [tʃuːz] v. 选择↔choice [tʃɔɪs] n. 选择

 $ \underline{\text{choose to make a choice to}} $ start a business  $ \underline{\text{选择}} $创业
 $ \underline{\text{choose}} $ between  $ \underline{\text{make a choice}} $ between family and career 在家庭和事业之间 $ \underline{\text{选择}} $
We  $ \underline{\text{cannot choose but}} $  $ \underline{\text{have no choice but to}} $ 或  $ \underline{\text{have no other choice than/except to}} $ equip ourselves with the ability to meet challenges.我们 $ \underline{\text{别无选择,只能}} $使自己具备迎接挑战的能力.

intend in'tend] v. 打算→intention in'tenʃn n. 打算
搭  $ \underline{\text{intend to}} $ study abroad↔with the intention of studying abroad 打算留学 have no/every intention of completing the assignments 毫无打算/一心只想完成任务

#### 2 动词↔形容词

Use your intellect to figure out what  $ \underline{\text{suits you best}} $ is most suitable for you 用理智来找出 $ \underline{\text{最适合你的}} $路
suit your needs/requirements/tastes 满足您的需要/要求/口味
a suitable place/time to meet 适合见面的地点/时间

diversity [daɪˈvɜːrsɪfaɪ] v. (使)多样化 → diverse [daɪˈvɜːrs] a. 多种多样的

搭 diversify the courses → provide diverse courses 使课程多样化

people from diverse cultures 来自不同文化(背景)的人

hold diverse views on this issue 在这一问题上持有不同的看法

tighten ['taɪtn] v. (使)变紧；使更加严格→tight [taɪt] a. 紧的；严格的
搭 tighten up on management → impose tight management 加强管理
tighten the grip on → keep a tight grip on sth 加强对某事的控制
a tight budget/schedule 紧张的预算/日程；a tight job market 严峻的就业市场

maximize  $ [maxismaiz] $ v. 使最大化  $ \leftrightarrow $ maximum  $ [maeksimam] $ a. 最大化的

摆 Only in this way can we maximize the benefit of online education  $ \leftrightarrow $ online education be of maximum benefit. 只有这样， $ \underline{\text{在线教育才能发挥最大效益}} $.
 $ \underline{\text{maximize<sup>↗</sup>make maximum use of}} $ opportunities  $ \underline{\text{充分利用}} $机会
develop our capabilities to the maximum 最大限度地发挥我们的能力
反 minimize the risks/damage/loss 将风险/伤害/损失降到最低
reduce screen time to the minimum 将屏幕(使用)时间减至最少

##### relate [ri'leɪt] v.<~ to>与……有关↔related [ri'leɪtɪd] a.相关的

 $ \underline{\text{closely relate to→be closely related to}} $ economic prosperity  $ \underline{\text{与经济繁荣密切相关}} $
The drop in the number of wild species was closely related to the growth of population. 野生物种数量的减少与人口增长密切相关.
related issues/fields 相关的问题/领域;career-related topics 职业相关的话题
 $ \underline{\text{联}} $ he connected with sth 与某物相关;connect A with B 将 A 与 B联系起来
be linked to sth 与某物相关;link A to/with B 将 A 与 B联系起来
be bound with/be tied up with sth 与某事物密切相关
A and B are interrelated/interconnected A 和 B 相互关联

#### 3 名词↔形容词

awareness [əˈweənəs] n.知道；意识←aware [əˈweə(r)] a.知道的；意识到的
 $ \underline{\text{have/develop an awareness of+be/become aware of}} $ the importance of self-confidence  $ \underline{\text{意识到}} $ 自信的重要性
raise/increase/heighten/enhance public awareness 增强公众的意识
there is a(n) growing/increasing awareness that... ……意识日益增强

##### access 「⌊ekses⌒ n.（接触的）机会↔accessible 「⌊k'sesəbl⌉ a.可/易接触的

people  $ \underline{\text{have/get/gain more access to}} $ higher education $ ^{①} $ higher education  $ \underline{\text{is more accessible to}} $ people 
人们 $ \underline{\text{有更多机会接受}} $高等教育
activities that provide access to the frontier areas of science and technology
能够使(人们)接触到科技前沿的活动
services/facilities that are easily/readily accessible to the public
公众很容易享受到的服务/可随时使用的设施

variety [vəˈraɪəti] n. 不同种类  $ \leftrightarrow $ various [ˈveəriəs] a. 各种各样的
 $ \underline{\text{a variety of←various}} $ activities  $ \underline{\text{各种各样的}} $活动
a wide variety of occupations 各行各业;a life full of variety 丰富多彩的生活

##### difficulty [ˈdɪfɪkəlti] n. 困难↔difficult [ˈdɪfɪkəlt] a. 困难的

 $ \underline{\text{꼼}} $  $ \underline{\text{find}} $ it  $ \underline{\text{difficult}} $ to  $ \underline{\text{land}} $  $ \rightarrow $  $ \underline{\text{have}} $  $ \underline{\text{difficulty}} $ (in)  $ \underline{\text{landing}} $ a decent job  $ \underline{\text{找}} $ 份好工作 $ \underline{\text{很难}} $ have difficulties with digital devices 在数字设备(的使用)方面有困难
run into/get into/experience/encounter difficulties 遭遇困难
overcome/resolve/conquer difficulties 克服/解决/战胜困难

importance [im'po:tns] n.重要性 $ \leftrightarrow $important [im'po:tnt] a.重要的

搭 be  $ \underline{\text{of importance}} $ $ \leftrightarrow $important 是 $ \underline{\text{重要的}} $
注:significance $ \leftrightarrow $significant、value $ \leftrightarrow $valuable、help $ \leftrightarrow $helpful、benefit $ \leftrightarrow $beneficial、necessity $ \leftrightarrow $necessary 等表抽象含义的组合中的名词适用于“be of+名词=形容词”的转换，名词前可增补 no、little、great、considerable 等修饰词，说明程度；名词后可增补 to sb/sth，引出对象

## 二、近/反义词的表达

1 表示增进、提升的动词：promote boost · enhance · strengthen · raise

##### boost「burst」v.使增长；使兴旺

 $ \underline{\text{揽}} $ boost one's confidence/ego/morale 增加信心/自尊/士气
boost the economy 促进经济增长;boost one's career 促进职业发展
boost one's efficiency/performance/competitiveness 提升效率/业绩/竞争力

enhance [ m'haɪns ] v. 提高；增强

搔 enhance the joy of learning 增添学习的乐趣

enhance understanding and friendship among countries and peoples

增进各国及各国人民之间的了解和友谊

strengthen [ˈstreŋ \theta n] v. 加强；增强

擂 strengthen the ties/bonds/links/relationships 加强联系

strengthen moral education 加强德育；strengthen the rule of law 加强法治

raise [ˈreɪz] v. 提高；提升

擂 raise one's spirits 打起精神；raise the standards of living 提高生活水平

raise one's hope 唤起希望；raise the academic standards 提高学术标准

2 表示削弱、降低的动词：decline · reduce weaken · undermine · lower

weaken [ˈwiːkən] v. (使)减弱，削弱

$\underline{\text{摟}} \) weaken sb's confidence/resolution 动摇某人的信心/决心

weaken the influence/power/position of sb 削弱某人的影响/权力/地位

undermine [ˌʌndərˈmaɪn] v. 逐渐削弱；暗中破坏

$\underline{\text{摟}} \) undermine trust and cooperation 破坏信任与合作

undermine the chances of success 降低成功的机会

lower ˈlʊər(r) 降低

$\underline{\text{摟}} \) lower prices 降低物价；lower the quality standards 降低质量标准

lower the threshold of starting a business 降低创业的门槛

③ 表示加重、加剧的动词：add worsen · aggravate · deteriorate

##### worsen [ˈwɜːsn] v. (使)恶化，加剧

搔 worsen the problem/situation 使问题/局势更糟
job prospects/relationships tend to worsen 就业前景/关系变得越来越糟

aggravate [ˈæɡrəveɪt] v. 使严重；使恶化

搭 aggravate the problem/situation 使问题/局势恶化

aggravate differences/tensions/conflicts 加剧分歧/紧张局势/冲突

deteriorate [ˈdɪˈtɪəriəreɪt] v. 恶化；退化

搭 deteriorating weather conditions/air quality/ecological environment

不断恶化的天气状况/空气质量/生态环境

#### 4 表示减轻、缓解的动词：ease lessen · relieve · alleviate

##### lessen ['lesn] v. (使)减弱，减轻

翟 lessen the pain/burden 减轻痛苦/负担

lessen the risk/possibility of conflict 降低冲突的风险/几率
relieve [rɪˈliːv] v. 减轻；缓和

relieve anxiety/guilt/stress/pressure 缓解忧虑/内疚/压力

relieve poverty/unemployment/traffic congestion

缓解贫困/失业/交通拥堵
alleviate [əˈlɪvieɪt] v. 减轻；缓解

alleviate the impact of a fast-paced lifestyle on health

减轻快节奏的生活方式给健康带来的影响

alleviate boredom/distress/depression/loneliness 缓解无聊/痛苦/郁闷/孤独

#### 5 表示扩大、扩展的动词：enlarge · widen · expand · extend

enlarge 「in'la:d3」v.(使)扩大，放大
 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ enlarge the recreation area/science museum/stadium
扩建娱乐场地/科技馆/体育场

widen [ˈwaɪdn] v. (使) 变宽，扩展 = broaden

搭 widen the gap/gulf/divide between... 扩大……之间的差距/隔阂/分歧

widen/broaden one's mind/horizons/knowledge 开阔思想/拓宽视野/拓展知识面

expand [ɪkˈspænd] v. 扩大(数量); 扩展(交际、业务等)

搭 expand the businesses/services/market 扩展业务/服务/市场

expand one's vocabulary 扩大词汇量; expand one's (social) circle 扩大交际圈

extend `rk'stend` v. 扩大(范围); 延长(期限)

擋 extend the application range 扩大应用范围

extend the deadline/visa/opening hours 延长最后期限/签证期限/营业时间

#### 6 表示获得、实现的动词：gain · achieve obtain · acquire · attain · realize · fulfill

obtain [əb'tein] v. (尤指经努力)获得,获取

搭 obtain the bachelor's/master's degree 获得学士/硕士学位
obtain information/permission/approval 获得信息/许可/批准

acquire [əˈkwɑɪə(r)] v. 获得(知识、技能等)；培养(习惯、品质)
搭 acquire knowledge 获得知识
acquire new/professional skills 获得新技能/专业技能

##### attain [əˈteɪn] v. (通过长时间努力) 获得；达到(某一境界)

揩 attain the highest grade 获得最高分；attain perfection 达到完美(的境地)

##### realize [ˈriːəlaɪz] v. 实现；将……变为现实

🏢 realize one's full potential 充分发挥潜力
realize one's dreams/ambitions/aspirations/goals 实现梦想/志向/抱负/目标

##### fulfill [fol'fil] v. 实现；符合；履行（英式拼写为 fulfil）

搭 fulfill one's role/duty/obligation/promise/pledge 履行职责/义务/诺言 fulfill oneself 实现自我价值; fulfill the requirement/need 符合要求/需要

#### 7 表示阻止、禁止的动词：stop prevent · forbid · ban · prohibit

prevent [prɪˈvent] v. 阻止；防止

撘 prevent accidents/pollution/brain drain 防止事故/污染/人才流失
prevent sb from engaging in unethical behavior 防止某人参与不道德的行为

##### forbid [fə'bid] v. 禁止；不准

撂 forbid minors to drink alcohol/from drinking alcohol 禁止未成年人饮酒

ban 「ban」 v. (以官方明令)禁止

搭 ban smoking in public places 禁止在公共场所吸烟

ban drivers from cell-phone use while driving 禁止司机在开车时使用手机

##### prohibit [prə'hɪbɪt] v. (以法令)禁止

撘 prohibit littering/treading on the lawn 禁止乱丢垃圾/践踏草坪

#### 8 表示惩罚、处罚的名词：fine · punishment · penalty

##### fine fan n. 罚金；罚款

搭 impose fines on owners who walk their dogs without a leash 对遛狗不牵绳者处以罚款 get heavy fines for discharging waste water into local rivers

因向当地河流排放污水被处以巨额罚款

##### punishment 「'panfmənt」n.惩罚；处罚

搭 impose a punishment on drunk drivers 对酒驾者施以处罚

receive harsh/severe punishments for school bullying/academic cheating

因校园暴力/学术造假行为而受到严厉惩罚

physical punishment 体罚；combine rewards with punishments 奖惩结合

##### penalty 「'penaltì」 n.（因违反法律、规则或合约而受到的）刑罚，罚款

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ impose heavy/harsh/severe penalties on tax evaders 对逃税者施以重罚 face penalties for neglecting children/abusing elderly people 因疏于照管儿童/虐待老人而面临处罚

#### 9 表示方式、方法的名词：way method · approach · means

method _ 'meθed_ n. (尤指熟知及经常使用的) 方法,办法

搭 a new method of/for solving the problem 解决问题的新方法

the teaching method 教学方法; the method of payment 支付方式

approach _ e'prəutf] n. (待人接物或处理问题的) 方式,方法

搭 an approach to raising children 育儿方法; a multi-pronged approach 多管齐下的办法

means [ mi:nz ] n. 方式; 手段

搭 a means of transport/communication 交通工具/交流方式

a means of assessing performance 评估表现的手段

#### 10 表示困难、阻碍的名词：difficulty hardship · obstacle · barrier

##### hardship [ˈhɑːdʃɪp] n. 艰难；困苦

撂 suffer/endure hardships 遭受/忍受困难；in times of hardship 在困难的时候

obstacle [ˈɒbstəkl] n. 障碍；阻碍 = hindrance
搔 an obstacle to building good habits 养成好习惯的阻碍
a(n) obstacle/hindrance to academic success 学业成功的阻碍
overcome/remove/eliminate/clear away an obstacle 克服/清除障碍

##### barrier ['baer(r)] n.障碍；隔阂

overcome/break down/tear down a barrier 克服/打破障碍
language/communication/cultural/geographical/technical/trade barriers
语言障碍/沟通障碍/文化隔阂/地理阻隔/技术阻碍/贸易壁垒

#### 11 表示巨大、大量的形容词：vast · massive · enormous · considerable · tremendous

##### vast vast a.（面积、数量等）巨大的；广阔的

搭 a vast amount of information 大量信息；a vast crowd 一大群人 vast knowledge 渊博的知识；the vast majority of...绝大多数……

##### massive  $ [^{1}massiv] $ u. (数额、规模等) 巨大的

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ massive debts 巨额的债务；massive destruction 大规模的破坏 a massive success/hit 巨大的成功；a massive blow 巨大的打击

##### enormous [ɪˈnɔːməs] a. (数量、兴趣、问题等) 巨大的 = immense

搭 enormous/immense interest/challenges 浓厚的兴趣/巨大的挑战 an enormous/immense amount of time and energy 大量的时间和精力

considerable [kənˈstɪdərəbl] a. 相当多(或大、重要等)的 = substantial 

 $ \underline{\text{搭}} $ considerable/substantial damage 巨大的伤害

a considerable/substantial achievement 重大的成就

tremendous [trə'mendəs] a. (尤指影响) 巨大的；极好的

搭 a tremendous experience/performance 极好的经历/精彩的表现

tremendous changes 巨变; a tremendous effect/impact/influence 巨大的影响

#### 12 表示重要、必要的形容词：vital · crucial · necessary · integral · indispensable

vital [ˈvaɪtl] a. 极为重要的；必不可少的 = essential

搭 be vital/essential to/for health 对于健康极为重要

##### crucial  $ ^{1} $kru:fl a.至关重要的；关键性的=critical

crucial kru:j1 a. 至关重要的；关键性的=critical

搭 be crucial/critical to our success 对于我们的成功至关重要

a crucial/critical factor/decision/moment 至关重要的因素/决定/时刻

搭 a necessary result/consequence 必然的结果

skills necessary for a fast-paced world 应对快速发展的世界所必备的技能

integral `intiqral` a. (用于构成整体)必需的，必不可少的

搭 an integral part of our daily lives 我们日常生活中必不可少的一部分

ndispensable $ ^{indispensabl} $ a. 不可或缺的；必不可少的

搭 be indispensable to our team 对于我们的团队不可或缺

be indispensable for achieving success 对于取得成功不可或缺

注：be of vital/essential/crucial/critical importance 至关重要 play a(n) vital/essential/crucial/critical/indispensable role 发挥重要/不可或缺的作用

#### 13 表示有用、有益的形容词：helpful beneficial · rewarding · conducive

##### rewarding [ri'wɔːdɪŋ] a.（活动等）有益的，值得做的；报酬高的

 $ \underline{\text{据}} $ be financially rewarding 经济回报丰厚的

a rewarding experience/job 有意义的经历/工作

conducive [kənˈdjuːsɪv] a. (常指环境、品质等) 有助于……的

搭 an environment conducive to learning 有助于学习的环境

#### 14 表示有害、无益的形容词：bad harmful · detrimental

harmful 'harmful a.(尤指对健康、环境等)有害的

据 be harmful to the environment 对环境有害；harmful habits 不良习惯

detrimental [ˈdetrɪmentl] a. 有害的；不利的 = damaging

搭 have a detrimental/damaging effect on wildlife 对野生动物有不利影响

be detrimental/damaging to our career advancement 不利于我们的事业发展

#### 16 表示突出、卓越的形容词：excellent striking · remarkable · outstanding

##### striking [ˈstræktɪŋ] a.（特征等）显著的，突出的 = marked

 $ \underline{\text{揸}} $ a striking feature 显著的特征; a striking example 突出的例子

a striking change/contrast/similarity/parallel 显著的变化/差异/相似性

remarkable [rɪˈmɑːkəbl] a.(成就等)显著的，非凡的

握 be remarkable for one's intelligence 才智出众

a remarkable achievement/accomplishment/feat 非凡的成就

make remarkable progress 取得显著进步；a remarkable event 引人瞩目的事件
outstanding [ˈaʊtˈstændɪŋ] a.出色的；杰出的

握 a(n) outstanding/distinguished/eminent/prominent scholar 杰出的学者

an outstanding example 杰出的典范；an outstanding performance 精彩的表现

## 第二节 句的多样化

## 一、句式变换

#### 1 从句或谓语部分变换为分词短语

(1)常规句: The GPA-based evaluation system which is implemented by educational institutions is culpable for fostering such inertia.

变换句: The GPA-based evaluation system implemented by educational institutions is culpable for fostering such inertia.

译文：教育机构推行的基于平均学分绩点的评价体系对于助长这种惰性难辞其咎。

(2)常规句: Such a tendency, if left as it is, will inevitably damage interpersonal relations over time, which will cause misunderstanding and distrust.

变换句: Such a tendency, if left as it is, will inevitably damage interpersonal relations over time, causing misunderstanding and distrust.

译文：这种趋势若继续发展下去，久而久之必然会破坏人际关系，导致误解与不信任

3 常规句: They fail to get their priorities right and easily fall into the vicious cycle of procrastination.

变换句1: Failing to get their priorities right, they easily fall into the vicious cycle of procrastination.

变换句2: They fail to get their priorities right, easily falling into the vicious cycle of procrastination.

译文：他们分不清事情的轻重缓急。(因而)容易陷入拖延的恶性循环中。

#### 2 从句变换为不定式短语

1. 常规句：There will always be obstacles that we must face and overcome on our way to success.

变换句：There will always be obstacles to face and overcome on our way to success.

译文：在我们通往成功的路上，总是会有阻碍要面对和克服。

2.常规句:I am pleased to offer several suggestions so that I could help you make a smooth transition to the campus life here.

变换句: To/In order to help you make a smooth transition to the campus life here, I am pleased to offer several suggestions.

译文：为了帮助你们顺利地向校园生活过渡，我很乐意提供几点建议。

#### 3 从句或谓语部分变换为形容词短语

(1) 常规句: This will equip us with various expertise and skills which are necessary for adapting to an increasingly competitive and ever-changing job market.

变换句: This will equip us with various expertise and skills necessary for adapting to an increasingly competitive and ever-changing job market.

译文：这将使我们具备各种必要的专业知识和技能以适应竞争越发激烈、变化越发迅猛的就业市场。

2常规句:In the left picture, a man is lolling back in his chair and is smug about a shelf full of books in front of him.

变换句: In the left picture, a man is lolling back in his chair, smug about a shelf full of books in front of him.

译文：左图中，一个人懒洋洋地靠在椅子上，望着眼前整整一书架的书沾沾自喜。

##### 从句或谓语部分变换为名词短语

常规句: The pictures highlight the significance of self-discipline, which is/and this is the ability to make ourselves do what we ought to do without being urged by someone else.

变换句: The pictures highlight the significance of self-discipline, the ability to make ourselves do what we ought to do without being urged by someone else.

译文：图片强调自律的重要性，即在没有他人敦促的情况下也能去做自己应该做的事。

#### 5 从句变换为介词短语

1. 常规句：Those who have an interdisciplinary background are more likely to stand out.

变换句：Those with an interdisciplinary background are more likely to stand out.

译文：拥有跨学科背景的人更有可能脱颖而出。

2 常规句: There is growing concern that smartphones have adverse effects on social life.

变换句: There is growing concern over the adverse effects of smartphones on social life.

译文：人们越来越担心智能手机对社交生活产生的负面影响。

#### 6 定语从句变换为名词性从句（此处特指主语/宾语/表语从句）

(1) 常规句: The thing that is needed is a sustained effort to conquer these obstacles.

变换句：What is needed is a sustained effort to conquer these obstacles.

译文：我们需要不懈的努力来克服这些障碍。

(2)常规句:I would like to offer some suggestions on the way in which you can find a job in China.

变换句:I would like to offer some suggestions on how you can find a job in China.

译文：针对如何在中国找工作，我想给你一些建议。

#### 7 肯定句变换为双重否定、意义肯定的句子

1 常规句: In the entertainment era, it is common for the young to idolize stars.

变换句: In the entertainment era, it is not uncommon for the young to idolize stars.

译文: 在娱乐时代，年轻人追星并不少见。

2. 常规句: We should realize the importance of knowledge across fields.

变换句: We should never underestimate the importance of knowledge across fields.

译文：我们绝不应低估跨领域知识的重要性。

3. 常规句: Something will be achieved if we can overcome inertia.

变换句: Nothing will be achieved without overcoming inertia.

译文：不克服惰性将一事无成。

#### 8 肯定句变换为形式否定、意义肯定的句子

1 常规句: The significance of self-discipline should be stressed.

变换句: The significance of self-discipline cannot be stressed enough.

译文：自律的重要性再怎么强调都不为过。

2.常规句:At such a tough moment, we can only grit our teeth.

变换句：At such a tough moment, we have no choice but to grit our teeth.

译文：在这样的艰难时刻，我们别无选择，只能咬紧牙关。

3 常规句：For some people, books are only decorations.

变换句: For some people, books are nothing but decorations.

译文：对有些人来说，书籍只不过是一种装饰。

4常规句: Perhaps family affection is the most important thing.

变换句：Perhaps nothing is more important than family affection.

译文：或许没有什么比亲情更重要

#### 9 否定句变换为形式肯定、意义否定的句子

1. 常规句：Parents should teach by example, not by command.

变换句: Parents should teach more by example than by command.

译文：父母应该更多地以身作则，而非只提要求。

2 常规句: These fervent fans have not realized that what deserves to be imitated is their idols' good behaviors.

变换句: These fervent fans have yet to realize that what deserves to be imitated is their idols' good behaviors.

译文: 这些疯狂的粉丝还未意识到值得他们效仿的是偶像的良好行为.

3常规句: We should never surrender our dreams for fear of disapproval from others.

变换句: The last thing we should do is (to) surrender our dreams for fear of disapproval from others.

译文：我们绝不应该因担心他人的反对而放弃自己的梦想。

## 二、特殊句型

#### 1 强调句

常规句: This experience opened his mind to a myriad of ideas.

变换句: It was this experience that opened his mind to a myriad of ideas.

译文：正是这段经历让他接触到了各种各样的观点。

#### 2 倒装句

(1)常规句: We can realize our personal ambitions only through constant efforts.

变换句: Only through constant efforts can we realize our personal ambitions.

译文：只有不断努力，我们才能实现自己的抱负

②常规句：I did not find your CD in my luggage until yesterday when I came to Beijing.

变换句：Not until yesterday when I came to Beijing did I find your CD in my luggage.

译文：直到昨天返回北京后，我才在行李箱里发现了你的CD.

3常规句: When we get closer to the finishing line, we feel more fatigued and lazier.

变换句: The closer we get to the finishing line, the more fatigued and lazier we feel.

译文：我们越接近终点线，就越会感到疲惫慵懒。

#### 3 it 充当形式主语的句子

(1) 常规句: To cultivate in ourselves this crucial habit is necessary if we want to achieve something impressive.

变换句: It is necessary (for us) to cultivate in ourselves this crucial habit if we want to achieve something impressive.

译文：但凡我们想有所作为，就有必要在自己身上培养这一关键的习惯。

2. 常规句: To require parents for their care and upbringing is our basic obligation.

变换句: It is our basic obligation to require parents for their care and upbringing.

译文：报答父母的养育之恩是我们应尽的基本义务。

③常规句：To shake off inertia takes a tremendous amount of self-discipline.

变换句：It takes a tremendous amount of self-discipline to shake off inertia.

译文：要摆脱惰性需要很强的自制力

#### 4 被动语态

(1) 常规句: We should see virtual life as a complement to real life.

变换句：Virtual life should be seen as a complement to real life.

译文：虚拟生活应被看作是现实生活的补充。

2常规句: Many people acknowledge that persistence is the key to success.

变换句: It is widely acknowledged that persistence is the key to success.

译文：人们普遍认为持之以恒是取得成功的关键。

#### 5 使用虚拟语气的句型

(1)常规句:Now we must take effective measures to tackle this issue.

变换句: It is high time we took/should take effective measures to tackle this issue.

译文：是时候采取有效措施来应对这一问题了

2常规句:Celebrities need to be well-mannered so as to set a good example to young people.

变换句：Celebrities need to be well-mannered lest they (should) set a poor example to young people.

译文：名人需要举止得当，以免为年轻人立下坏榜样。

# 第四单元 热点话题预测

## 一、商业经济

#### 1. 行业发展

#### ·行业门类·

agriculture [ˈæɡrɪkʌltʃə(r)] n. 农业；农学

wholesaling ['həʊlsɛlɪŋ] n. 批发业

manufacturing _mænju'fæktʃərɪŋ] n. 制造业

#### 经济模式

logo ['ləʊgəʊ] n. 标识；标志

import 'import'] n.进口;输入

#### · 客户服务 ·

coupon [ˈkuːpən] n. 配给券：优惠券

### 发展趋势

bubble [ˈbʌbl] n. 泡沫；(持续不长的)好景

deficit ['defisit] n. 赤字；逆差

revival [riˈvaɪvl] n. 振兴；复苏

deflation [ ,dir'fleifn ] n.通货紧缩

inflation [ɪnˈfleɪʃn] n. 通货膨胀

recession [riˈseʃn] n. 经济衰退

standstill ['stændstɪl] n. 停顿；停滞

economic stability 经济稳定

economic slowdown 经济放缓

economic prospect/outlook 经济前景

boom-bust cycle 经济的盛衰周期

seasonal fluctuation 季节性波动

innovation-driven development 创新驱动型发展

long-term stability and prosperity 长期稳定繁荣

#### 2. 交易活动

reservation [rezə'veifn] n.预订；预约

transaction [trænˈzækʃn] n. 交易；业务

group buying 团购

sales return 销售退货

free delivery 免费送货

mortgage payment 按揭付款

early bird discount 早鸟折扣

special offer/order 特价优惠/特别定制

value-added service 增值服务

## 六、个人发展

#### 1. 品质精神

brilliance ['brliəns] n. 才能；才华

###### a. 受大风吹的

在40英亩向风的土地上漫步

扩 the windswept Atlantic coast 受大风侵袭的大西洋海岸 a beautiful windswept hillside 一处景色优美的向风山坡

近 windblown [ˈwɪndbləʊn] a. 被风吹的

## （四）副词（1词）

viscerally $ ^{2} $ ★☆☆ [ˈvɪsərəli]

ad. 发自肺腑地；出自内心地

真 hate photographs of oneself viscerally

打心眼里反感自己的照片

make sb viscerally angry

让某人发自内心地生气

understand viscerally for the first time the risks

sb faces

第一次发自内心地理解某人所面临的危机
